–°–µ—Ä–≥–µ–π 
function add_to_actor_pstor(npc_id)
  local actor=db.actor
  --mylog("add to pstor")
  if actor then
    local nid=npc_id
    if actor_team_ids then
      actor_team_ids[nid]=true
    end
    local cnt=xr_logic.pstor_retrieve(actor,"team_cnt",0)
    local firstzero=0
    for i=1,cnt,1 do
      if xr_logic.pstor_retrieve(actor,"team_id_"..i,0)==nid then
      -- —É–∂–µ –≤ –∫–æ–º–∞–Ω–¥–µ
        return
      elseif xr_logic.pstor_retrieve(actor,"team_id_"..i,0)==0 and firstzero==0 then
        firstzero=i
      end
    end
    if firstzero==0 then
      cnt=cnt+1
      xr_logic.pstor_store(actor,"team_cnt",cnt)
    else
      cnt=firstzero
    end
    -- --mylog("adding spot for member "..cnt)
    local npc=level.object_by_id(nid)
    -- level.map_add_object_spot_ser(nid, "anh_merc", (npc or "–ù–∞—ë–º–Ω–∏–∫") and npc:character_name())
    xr_logic.pstor_store(actor,"team_id_" .. cnt,nid)
  else
    -- --mylog("db.actor is nil in add_to_actor_pstor!")
  end
end

function is_companion(npc_id)
        if npc_id then
                if companions[npc_id] and companions[npc_id] == "companion" then
                        return true
                end
        end
        return false
end
